#### Absorb
___
- **Type:** Grass
- **Move Power:** Wisdom/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 20 feet
- **Description:**  
You attempt to absorb some of an enemy’s health. Make a ranged attack on a creature. On a hit, the creature takes 1d4 + MOVE grass damage. Half the damage done is restored by the user.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d4 at level 5, 3d4 at level 11, and 4d4 at level 17.

#### Accelerock
___
- **Type:** Rock
- **Move Power:** Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 6
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
Faster than a blink of an eye, you smack the opponent with a bit of rock. You may move up to your speed and make a melee attack. On a hit, the Pokémon takes 1d4 + MOVE rock damage
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d6 at level 5, 1d10 at level 11, and 2d8 at level 17.

#### Acid
___
- **Type:** Poison
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You create a stream of hot acid and aim it at your enemy. Make a ranged attack roll, doing 1d6 + MOVE poison damage on a hit.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d6 at level 5, 3d6 at level 11, and 4d6 at level 17.

#### Acid Armor
___
- **Type:** Poison
- **Move Power:** Constitution
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You are surrounded by a shield of thick acid for the duration. During this time, your AC increases by 2, and any Pokémon that hits you with a melee attack takes 1d8 poison damage.
- **Higher Levels:**  
Poison damage increases to 2d8 At level 10.

```
```

#### Acid Spray
___
- **Type:** Poison
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self (15-foot cone)
- **Description:**  
You spit a spray of acid in a 15 foot cone originating from yourself. Each creature in the area must make a Constitution saving throw against your MOVE DC. On a failure the creature takes 2d4 poison damage and has disadvantage on its next saving throw. On a success they take half damage and do not get the disadvantage on their saving throw.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 4d4 at level 5, 6d4 at level 11, and 8d4 at level 17.

#### Acrobatics
___
- **Type:** Flying
- **Move Power:** Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You move through the battlefield, making a quick succession of strikes. When you use this action you do not take attacks of opportunity until the end of your turn. You may make three melee attacks against different targets as you move. Each attack does 1d6 + MOVE flying damage.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d10 at level 5, 2d6 at level 11, and 2d10 at level 17.

#### Acupressure
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You use a secret technique to calm and cleanse yourself. When you use this move you can end one effect on yourself that is causing you to be charmed, frightened, paralyzed, poisoned, flinched, or stunned.

\page

<div class='pageNumber auto'></div>

#### Aerial Ace
___
- **Type:** Flying
- **Move Power:** Strength/Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
From the air you slash into and through the target. If you can be airborne this turn, make a melee attack with advantage doing 1d6+MOVE flying damage.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d6 at level 5, 3d6 at level 11, and 4d6 at level 17.

#### After You
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 2
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Description:**  
You politely let your ally take the initiative. Choose a willing creature that you can see within range. Until the spell ends, the target's speed is doubled, it gains a +2 bonus to AC, it has advantage on Dexterity saving throws, and gains an additional action on each of its turns. That action can only be used to take the Dash, Disengage, Hide or Use an Object action. When this move ends, the target can't move or take actions until after its next turn.

#### Agility
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 30 seconds
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You hone in on your abilities and feel a surge of speed course through your veins. As long as you have the type, increase your walking, flying, or swimming speed by 20 feet for the duration. You can only increase each type of your speed by 20 feet total with this move.

```
```

#### Air Cutter
___
- **Type:** Flying
- **Move Power:** Dexterity/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**  
You send a razor sharp slice of air towards your opponent. Make a ranged attack roll against an opponent dealing 1d6 + MOVE flying damage on a hit. This move crits on a natural roll of 19 or 20.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d6 at level 5, 3d6 at level 11, and 4d6 at level 17.

#### Air Slash
___
- **Type:** Flying
- **Move Power:** Wisdom/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**  
You conjure up a powerful slice of compacted air and hurl it at an enemy Pokémon. Make a ranged attack roll, doing 1d8 + MOVE flying damage on a successful hit. If the natural roll for this attack is 18 or higher, the target becomes flinched.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d8 at level 5, 3d8 at level 11, and 4d8 at level 17.

#### Ally Switch
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 6
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 100 feet
- **Description:**  
You use your psychic abilities to teleport yourself and an ally. Pick one willing creature within range. You and that creature swap positions. If either you or your target is too large to fit in their new spot, this move does nothing.

#### Amnesia
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 1 minute
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
Your mind elevates to a new level of focus. Add +5 to any saving throw you make for the duration, but select one of your other moves. You forget that move and cannot use it for the duration. You cannot have the bonus from amnesia more than once.

#### Anchor Shot
___
- **Type:** Steel
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Description:**  
You fire an anchor attached to a chain straight at your opponent. Make a ranged attack roll at your opponent, dealing 1d10 steel damage on a hit. If you hit this attack you may choose immediately pull your target up to 10 feet towards yourself.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d10 at level 5, 3d10 at level 11, and 4d10 at level 17.

#### Ancient Power
___
- **Type:** Rock
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 80 feet
- **Description:**  
You levitate a pile of earth and crush an enemy Pokémon with it. Make a ranged attack roll, doing 1d8 + MOVE rock damage on a successful hit.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d8 at level 5, 3d8 at level 11, and 4d8 at level 17.

#### Aqua Jet
___
- **Type:** Water
- **Move Power:** Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 6
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You surround yourself in a stream of water which lets you speed through battle. You may move up to your speed and make a melee attack. On a hit, the Pokémon takes 1d4 + MOVE water damage.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d6 at level 5, 1d10 at level 11, and 2d8 at level 17.

#### Aqua Ring
___
- **Type:** Water
- **Move Power:** Constitution/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
Rings of healing water surround you. While the rings exist, you heal 1d4 + MOVE each turn at the end of your turn.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d6 at level 5, 1d8 at level 11, and 1d10 at level 17.

#### Aqua Tail
___
- **Type:** Water
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You surround your tail with a whirling current and slam it into our foe. Make a melee attack roll against an opponent, dealing 1d10 + MOVE water damage on a hit.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d10 at level 5, 3d10 at level 11, and 4d10 at level 17.

#### Arm Thrust
___
- **Type:** Fighting
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You thrust out an open hand and unleash relentless strikes against a Pokémon. Make a melee attack roll, doing 1d6 + MOVE on a hit. After successfully hitting a target, roll a d4. On a result of 3 or 4, you may immediately hit again for an additional 1d6 normal damage. Continue this process until you fail to roll a 3 or 4 on the d4 roll.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d8 at level 5, 1d10 at level 11, and 1d12 at level 17.

\page

<div class='pageNumber auto'></div>

#### Aromatherapy
___
- **Type:** Grass
- **Move Power:** Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
A sweet refreshing wind gently blows. This Pokémon makes a medicine check. If the result of the check is higher than the DC to remove a status effect on any creature within 60 feet (line of sight) from the caster, the effect is removed. If there is no DC to remove the status effect, the effective DC is 15.

#### Aromatic Mist
___
- **Type:** Fairy
- **Move Power:** Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Self (20-foot sphere)
- **Description:**  
You exude a sweet perfume, bolstering your ally's resolve. For the duration of this move whenever you or a friendly creature within 20 feet of you makes a saving throw, the creature gains a bonus to the saving throw equal to your Charisma modifier (with a minimum bonus of +1).

#### Astonish
___
- **Type:** Ghost
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 20
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Description:**  
You make a face or feint a movement. If the target can see you, it must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or take 1d4 ghost damage and become flinched.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d4 at level 5, 3d4 at level 11, and 4d4 at level 17.

#### Assist
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 hour
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You try to be as helpful as possible. For the duration you can use the help action as a bonus action.

```
```

#### Assurance
___
- **Type:** Dark
- **Move Power:** Strength/Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 6
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You slap your opponent on the back, making sure they know you'll be there for them (when they die, cause you're killing them). Make a melee attack roll against your opponent, dealing 1d6  + MOVE damage on a hit. If you directly damaged your target since the start of your previous turn, you have advantage on the attack roll.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d6 at level 5, 3d6 at level 11, and 4d6 at level 17.

#### Attack Order
___
- **Type:** Bug
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 45 feet
- **Description:**  
You send out your swarm in a vicious biting, stinging attack. Make a ranged attack roll, dealing 1d10 bug damage on a hit. This move lands a critical hit on an attack roll of 19 or 20.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d10 at level 5, 3d10 at level 11, and 4d10 at level 17.

#### Attract
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** 10 minutes
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You are the cutest. One creature of a gender different than yours within range must succeed Charisma saving throw or be charmed for the duration, or until you or your companions do anything harmful to it.

#### Aura Sphere
___
- **Type:** Fighting
- **Move Power:** Strength/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 6
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**  
You gather your spirit in a compact ball of energy and fire it at an enemy. Make a ranged attack roll with advantage, doing 1d12 + MOVE fighting damage on a successful hit.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d12 at level 5, 3d12 at level 11, and 4d12 at level 17.

#### Aurora Beam
___
- **Type:** Ice
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self (60-foot line)
- **Description:**  
You create a 60-foot long, 5-foot wide line of glowing but freezing cold light. Any creature caught in the line must make a dexterity saving throw, taking 2d6 ice damage on a failure or half as much on a success. If a creature fails the saving throw by 10 or more, it becomes frozen.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 4d6 at level 5, 6d6 at level 11, and 8d6 at level 17.

#### Aurora Veil
___
- **Type:** Ice
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 1 hour
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You surround yourself with a dancing veil of rainbow lights. You gain 5 temporary hit points for the duration. If a creature hits you with a melee attack while you have those temporary hit points, the creature takes 5 ice damage.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The temporary health and ice damage of this move increase to 15 at level 5, 25 at level 11, and 35 at level 17.

```
```

#### Autotomize
___
- **Type:** Steel
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You sharpen your mind and feel a surge of power throughout you. As long as you have the type, increase your walking, flying, or swimming speed by 20 feet for the duration. You deal an extra 1d4 on melee attacks for the duration.
- **Higher Levels:**  
At level 10 the extra damage on your melee attacks increases to 2d4.

#### Avalanche
___
- **Type:** Ice
- **Move Power:** Strength/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You unleash a torrent of ice and snow that was loosened by a violent act. Target a space within range. Draw a line from that space 5 feet wide and 20 feet long. Any creature caught in the line must succeed on a DEX saving throw against your Move DC, taking 2d6 ice damage on a failed save, or half damage on a success. If you are below half HP, those creatures have disadvantage on the saving throw.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 4d6 at level 5, 6d6 at level 11, and 8d6 at level 17.

#### Baby Doll Eyes
___
- **Type:** Fairy
- **Move Power:** Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 reaction
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
As your opponent strikes out towards you, you give them big puppy-dog eyes. After an attack roll against you is declared but before the roll is made you can use your reaction to cause one enemy to make a Charisma saving throw against you MOVE DC. On a failure that creature has disadvantage on the attack. If that attack hits, you only take half damage.

<div class='pageNumber auto'></div>

#### Baneful Bunker
___
- **Type:** Poison
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 reaction
- **PP:** 6
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You arm your poison spikes and point them toward your foe. As a reaction when you are targeted by an attack you may increase your AC by +5 until the start of your next turn. You must decide to to use this move before you know if the triggering attack hits. If your attacker is adjacent to you when you use this move and their attack misses, your attacker becomes poisoned.

#### Barrage
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Strength/Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Description:**  
Make a ranged attack on a Pokémon. If you hit, roll 1d4. You attack with a barrage of ranged strikes equal to the number shown. Make a ranged attack roll for each projectile. The projectiles do 1d4 normal damage each on a hit.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d6 at level 5, 1d8 at level 11, and 1d10 at level 17.

#### Barrier
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You create a transparent shield of psychic energy. For the duration, the barrier grants +2 to AC for you and any allies within a 5 foot radius of you.

#### Baton Pass
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Touch
- **Description:**  
You pass on your energy to another. Choose one target you can touch. You may give your action to the target, losing your action this turn and gaining the target an extra action to use on their turn. You cannot use this move if you have already used your action this turn. Once you use this move your turn ends immediately.

```
```

#### Beak Blast
___
- **Type:** Flying
- **Move Power:** Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 1 round (Concentration)
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You gather a ferocious energy inside your beak, preparing to unleash it in a blast. During the duration, if you are hit by an opponent that is adjacent to you, that opponent becomes burned. As your next turn's action, if you keep your concentration, you unleash your stored energy. Make a range attack roll against one opponent with range, dealing 5d6 +MOVE damage on a hit.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 8d6 at level 5, 11d6 at level 11, and 14d6 at level 17.

#### Beat Up
___
- **Type:** Dark
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 8
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You call upon the strength of your allies to gang up on an enemy. Make a melee attack roll against an opponent. On a successful hit you deal 1d4 dark damage per Pokeslot your trainer has access to, then adding your MOVE modifier for additional dark damage. A wild Pokémon does 1d4 dark damage per active ally adjacent to itself up to a maximum of 6d4, then adds their MOVE modifier.

#### Belch
___
- **Type:** Poison
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 7
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Description:**  
You release a horrendous belch of digestive gases. Make a ranged attack against an opponent dealing 1d4 + MOVE poison damage on a hit. If you have eaten a berry during this combat, all the damage die for this move become d12s.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d4 at level 5, 3d4 at level 11, and 4d4 at level 17.

<div class='pageNumber auto'></div>

#### Belly Drum
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You begin to beat your stomach and throw yourself into a battle dance. Your next successful attack does 1d6 normal damage to yourself and 2d6 extra normal damage to the target.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The damage to you and the opponent increases to 2d6 and 4d6 respectively at 5th level, 3d6 and 6d6 at 11th level, and 4d6 and 8d6 at 17th level.

#### Bestow
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You use your natural affinity for others to assist in battle. For the duration, your friends have advantage on melee attack rolls against any creature within 5 feet of you that is hostile to you.

#### Bide
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Strength/Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Description:**  
You embrace the damage done to you, waiting for your time to strike. You may use your action to activate this move and keep track of all damage done to you before your next turn. On your next turn, you may use your action to lash out an an enemy with a ranged attack, striking them for double the amount of damage you took since your last turn on a successful hit.
- **Higher Levels:**  
At 11th Level, you can choose to hold Bide for a second turn for the chance to add additional damage to the attack.

```
```

#### Bind
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You attempt to grapple a target into submission. Make a melee attack roll. On a hit, the target takes 1d6 + MOVE normal damage and becomes grappled and restrained. At the beginning of each of its turns, it may attempt to escape with a Strength saving throw against your Move DC. While a Pokémon is grappled by you, you may continue to do an automatic 1d6 + MOVE damage as a bonus action and without using PP.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage increases to 1d12 at level 11.

#### Bite
___
- **Type:** Dark
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You sink your teeth into an enemy Pokémon. Make a melee attack roll, doing 1d6 + MOVE dark damage on a successful hit.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d6 at level 5, 3d6 at level 11, and 4d6 at level 17.

#### Blast Burn
___
- **Type:** Fire
- **Move Power:** Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 2
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**  
You decimate your foe with a powerful explosion of fire. Make a ranged attack roll doing 8d8 fire damage on a hit. Until the end of your next turn, your movement speed becomes zero and you cannot use damaging moves.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The damage increases to 12d8 at level 11.

<div class='pageNumber auto'></div>

#### Blaze Kick
___
- **Type:** Fire
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You ignite your foot with fire and kick your target. Make a melee attack roll, doing 1d8 + MOVE fire damage on a successful hit. This move crits on a natural roll of 19 or 20. If you hit your target must make a DC 10 Constitution saving throw or become burned.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d8 at level 5, 3d8 at level 11, and 4d8 at level 17.

#### Blizzard
___
- **Type:** Ice
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**  
Icy clouds form overhead and pelt the ground with hail and snow, centered on a point you choose within range. Each Pokémon within a 10 foot radius must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Move DC, taking 4d6 ice damage on a failed save, or half as much on a successful one.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 7d6 at level 5, 10d6 at level 11, and 13d6 at level 17.

#### Block
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Touch
- **Description:**  
By forcing your body in front of your foe, you stop their movement. Choose one opponent within range to make a Strength saving throw. On a failure they become restrained (though nothing is physically holding them). The target can retry the saving throw at the end of its turn to break the effect.

```
```

#### Body Slam
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 6
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You thrust yourself towards an opponent in an attempt to crush them with your physical size. Make a melee attack on a target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 + MOVE normal damage, and must succeed on a DC 12 Constitution saving throw or become paralyzed.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d8 at level 5, 3d8 at level 11, and 4d8 at level 17.

#### Bone Club
___
- **Type:** Ground
- **Move Power:** Strength/Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You strike a Pokémon with a club of bone. Make a melee attack roll, doing 1d8 + MOVE on a successful hit. If the natural attack roll is 18 or more, the target flinches on their next turn.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of the attack increases to 1d10 at level 5, and 1d12 at level 11. The flinch range increases to 17 or more at level 5 and 16 or more at level 11.

#### Bone Rush
___
- **Type:** Ground
- **Move Power:** Strength/Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
A spectral bone appears in your hand. You make a series of quick attacks with it before it disappears. Make a melee attack roll, doing 1d6 + MOVE on a hit. After successfully hitting a target, roll a d4. On a result of 3 or 4, you may immediately hit again for an additional 1d6 ground damage. Continue this process until you fail to roll a 3 or 4 on the d4 roll.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d8 at level 5, 1d10 at level 11, and 1d12 at level 17.

\page

<div class='pageNumber auto'></div>

#### Bonemerang
___
- **Type:** Ground

#### Curse
___
- **Type:** Ghost
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 4
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You twist fates and throw a curse on the battle. You touch a creature, and that creature must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become cursed for the Duration of the spell. When you cast this spell, choose the nature of the curse from the following options. • Choose one ability score. While cursed, the target has disadvantage on Ability Checks and Saving Throws made with that ability score. • While cursed, the target has disadvantage on Attack rolls against you. • While cursed, the target must make a Wisdom saving throw at the start of each of its turns. If it fails, it wastes its action that turn doing nothing. • While the target is cursed, your attacks deal an extra 1d8 necrotic damage to the target.
- **Higher Levels:**  
At level 5 the duration increases to 10 minutes (Concentration), at 11th level the duration increases to 8 hours (Concentration), and at 17th level the duration increases to 24 hours (Concentration).

#### Defog
___
- **Type:** Flying
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 15
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
A line of strong wind 60 feet long and 10 feet wide blasts from you in a direction you choose for the spell's duration. Each creature that starts its turn in the line must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pushed 15 feet away from you in a direction following the line. Any creature in the line must spend 2 feet of movement for every 1 foot it moves when moving closer to you.The gust disperses gas or vapor, and it extinguishes candles, torches, and similar unprotected flames in the area. It causes protected flames, such as those of lanterns, to dance wildly and has a 50 percent chance to extinguish them. As a bonus action on each of your turns before the spell ends, you can change the direction in which the line blasts from you. This move removes hazards from the field.

#### Disable
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Charisma/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**

Each of the opponent’s moves is numbered 1 – 4 in alphabetical order. The move corresponding to the number rolled is unable to be activated for one minute. If the number rolled is higher than the number of moves known by the target Pokémon, reroll the d4 until you get a lower result. A single Pokémon cannot have more than one moved disabled in this way.

#### Explosion
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Strength/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 1
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self (5-foot sphere)
- **Description:**  
You make yourself a sphere of energy that packs a concentrated and devastating explosion. Each Pokémon with a sphere of 5 foot radius centered on yourself makes a Dexterity saving throw against you MOVE DC. On a failed save they take normal damage equal to 1d20 per every 3 levels of the exploding Pokémon (for example, doing 3d20 damage at level 9,10, and 11). On a successful save they take no damage. The user is reduced to 0 HP and falls unconscious after using this move.

- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You reach out and unleash relentless strikes against a Pokémon. Make a melee attack roll, doing 1d6 + MOVE normal damage on a hit. After successfully hitting a target, roll a d4. On a result of 3 or 4, you may immediately hit again for an additional 1d6 normal damage. Continue this process until you fail to roll a 3 or 4 on the d4 roll.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d8 at level 5, 1d10 at level 11, and 1d12 at level 17.

#### Future Sight
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
By focus your psychic abilities you receive an omen about the results of a specific course of action that you plan to take within the next 30 minutes. The DM chooses from the following possible omens.  • Weal, for good results  • Woe, for bad results  • Weal and woe, for both good and bad results  • Nothing, for results that aren't especially good or bad  This move doesn't take into account any possible circumstances that might change the outcome, such as the use of addition moves or the loss or gain of a companion. If you use this move two or more times before completing your next Long Rest, there is a cumulative 25 percent chance for each use after the first that you get a random reading. The DM makes this roll in secret.

#### Gravity
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** Intelligence
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 1
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** 100 feet
- **Description:**  
This move reverses gravity in a 50-foot-radius, 100-foot high Cylinder centered on a point within range. All creatures and Objects that aren't somehow anchored to the ground in the area fall upward and reach the top of the area when you cast this spell. A creature can make a Dexterity saving throw against you MOVE DC to grab onto a fixed object it can reach, thus avoiding the fall. If some solid object (such as a ceiling) is encountered in this fall, falling objects and creatures strike it just as they would during a normal downward fall. If an object or creature reaches the top of the area without striking anything, it remains there, oscillating slightly, for the Duration. At the end of the Duration, affected objects and creatures fall back down.

#### Growl
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 minute
- **Range:** 100 feet
- **Description:**  
You target a Pokémon with an intimidating growl. The Pokémon must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Move DC. On a fail, it adds -2 to any attack it makes for the duration. This modifier can be stacked if it fails multiple growl saves, up to a maximum of -4.

#### Growth
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Touch
- **Description:**  
The target's size doubles in all dimensions, and its weight is multiplied by eight. This growth increases its size by one category - from Medium to Large, for example. If there isn't enough room for the target to double its size, the creature or object attains the maximum possible size in the space available. Until the spell ends, the target also has advantage on Strength Checks and Strength saving throws. The targets' attacks with any enlarged appendage deal 1d4 extra damage.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The extra damage dice increases to 1d6 at level 10

#### Grudge
___
- **Type:** Ghost
- **Move Power:** Wisdom/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 reaction
- **PP:** 4
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 1000 feet
- **Description:**  
Your hate for the opponent allows you to get the last laugh. When an opposing Pokémon within range damages you, you may use your reaction to use Grudge. If you die or faint because of the damage from the move that caused you to activate Grudge, the Pokémon that used that damaging move must make a Wisdom saving throw at disadvantage. On a failure, that Pokémon loses all PP from the move that killed or knocked you out. You must choose to use Grudge before the damage total from the attacking move is known.

- **Range:** 50 feet
- **Description:**

That warded creature only takes half damage from all wounds and attacks that deal hit point damage. The amount of damage not taken by the warded creature is taken by you. If you and the subject of the spell move out of range of each other, the spell ends.

- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** 150 feet

- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You inspire your teammates to do their best. To use this move choose one creature other than yourself within 60 feet of you who can see you. That creature gains one inspiration die, a 1d6. Once within the next 10 minutes, the creature can roll the die and add the number rolled to one ability check, attack roll, or saving throw it makes. the creature can wait until after it rolls the d20 before deciding to use the inspiration die, but must decide before the DM says whether the roll succeeds or fails. Once the inspiration die is rolled, it is lost. A creature can have only one inspiration die at a time.

___
- **Type:** Ghost
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 hour (Concentration)
- **Range:** 90 feet
- **Description:**

The base damage of this attack increases to 1d10 at level 5, 2d6 at level 11, and 2d10 at level 17.

#### Hurricane
___
- **Type:** Flying
- **Move Power:** Wisdom/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 2
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**  
You conjure an spiraling cylinder of wind in range, which has a 20 foot radius and 40 foot height. This cylinder becomes difficult terrain for the duration, even for flying creatures. When a creature enters the spell’s area for the first time on a turn or starts its turn there, it is buffeted by high winds and it must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Move DC. If it fails, it takes 4d6 flying damage on a failed save, and half as much on a successful one. If a creature rolls a natural 1 on the save, they become confused. On each of your turns after you cast this spell, you can use an action to move the storm 30 feet in any direction.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 6d6 at level 5, 8d6 at level 11, and 10d6 at level 17.

#### Infestation
___
- **Type:** Bug
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** 20 feet
- **Description:**

On a failed save the target is additionally infested for 2d4 bug damage at the start of each of its subsequent turns. Only one Pokémon can be infested by you at a time.

The base damage of this attack increases to 2d6 at level 5, 2d8 at level 11, and 2d10 at level 17.

#### Magic Coat
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 reaction
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Description:**  
You surround yourself in a bouncy protective sheen. On a failure, they receive the status. This move can only reflect status effects. If a saving throw would cause you to take a status condition in addition some other effect, you may still cause your attacker to attempt their own saving throw to take the status effect but you also must make the saving throw and accept the other effects as per your result.

- **PP:** 4
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 80 feet
- **Description:**  
You send a chilling, spectral wind through your opponents. Choose a point within range. Each creature within a 30 foot cube centered on that point must make a Constitution saving throw or take 3d6 ghost damage on a failed save or half as much on a successful save. If you roll maximum damage on any of the damage die for this attack any creatures who failed their saving throw also become frightened of you for 1 minute. A frightened creature can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on itself on a success. If a creature's saving throw is successful or the effect ends for it, the creature is immune to being frightened by your Ominous Wind for 24 hours.

- **Type:** Rock
- **Move Power:** Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You turn the ground around you into 3 large boulders and fling them to make a tomb. Each boulder is approximately a 5 foot diameter, 10 foot tall cylinder. The boulders must be placed so that each boulder touches the previous boulder starting from a point within range and never going out of range. If a boulder would take up a space that a creature is in that creature is pushed to one side of the boulder (your choice). Any creature affect in this way must make a Dexterity saving throw against your MOVE DC, falling prone on a failure.
- **Higher Levels:**  
At level 5 you can creature a total of 4 boulders, at level 11 you can creature a total of 5 boulders, and at level 17 you can create a total of 6 boulders.

- **Duration:** 10 minutes (Concentration)
- **Range:** 100 feet
- **Description:**

If a creature is concentrating in the sandstorm when this move is used, it must make a Constitution save to maintain it. #### Seed Bomb
___
- **Type:** Grass
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 10 minutes (Concentration)
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**  
You imbue a seed with a magic energy before lobbing it to deliver the package. The ground in a 20-foot radius centered on a point within range twists and sprouts hard spikes and thorns. The area becomes difficult terrain for the duration. When a creature moves into or within the area, it takes 2d4 grass damage for every 5 feet it travels. The transformation of the ground is camouflaged to look natural. Any creature that can't see the area at the time the spell is cast must make a Wisdom (Perception) check against your MOVE DC to recognize the terrain as hazardous before entering it.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The damage done per 5 feet of movement through the area of seed bomb increases to 4d4 at level 11

- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**

#### Self Destruct
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Strength/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 1
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self (10-foot sphere)
- **Description:**

If your Pokémon has at least half its hit points left, anyone in range takes 8d6 normal damage on a failed save or half as much on a successful one. If your Pokémon has less than half of its hit points left, the damage is halved again for both a successful and unsuccessful saving throw. The user is reduced to 0 HP and falls unconscious after using this move.

The base damage of this attack increases to 8d8 at level 5, 8d10 at level 11, and 8d12 at level 17.

#### Skill Swap
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** Intelligence
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 10 minutes (Concentration)
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You create a psychic link with another creature. Target one other creature to make a Intelligence saving throw against your MOVE DC. On a failed save you can pick one of their abilities to use for yourself (if they have any). You must then allow the creature to use one of your abilities. During this time neither of you can use the ability you traded away. You each can use each others abilities until Skill Swap ends, at which point they return to their original owners.

- **Description:**

Any creature who moves through the field takes 1d4 damage per five feet they move. If a creature is expelled from their Pokeball onto the field, they take twice the normal amount of damage.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d6 at level 5, 2d4 at level 11, and 2d6 at level 17.

#### Stealth Rock
___
- **Type:** Rock
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You break off a few sharp shards of rock, which begin to levitate around you. You create 3 shards which float around you until you trigger them. When you are hit by an attack you may use your reaction to interpose shards between yourself and the attack. For each shard you use in this way you gain +1 AC versus the triggering attack. Using the shards in this way does not destroy them. On your turn, you can direct the shards to attack an adjacent opponent as a bonus action. Make a single melee attack roll against that opponent. On a hit you deal 1d4+1 points of rock damage for each shard you used to attack. Once a shard damages an opponent in this way, your link with it dissipates and you can no longer control it for this use of Stealth Rock.
- **Higher Levels:**  
At 5th level the number of shards you make increases to 4, at 11th level the number increases to 5, and at 17th level it increases to 6.

#### Sticky Web
___
- **Type:** Bug
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 hour (Concentration)
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You conjure a mass of thick, sticky webbing at a point of your choice within range. The webs fill a 20-foot cube from that point for the duration. The webs are difficult terrain and lightly obscure their area. Webs layered over a flat surface have a depth of 5 feet. Each creature that starts its turn in the webs or that enters them during its turn must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, the creature is restrained as long as it remains in the webs or until it breaks free. A creature restrained by the webs can use its actions to make a Strength check against your MOVE DC. If it succeeds, it is no longer Restrained. The webs are flammable. Any 5-foot cube of webs exposed to fire burns away in 1 round, dealing 2d4 fire damage to any creature that starts its turn in the fire.

#### Stockpile
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 15
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You create in your stomach a stockpile of flem and digested materials. You add a stack of Stockpile to yourself. You can have up to 5 stacks of Stockpile at one time. For each stack of Stockpile you have, you gain +1 AC. When you use Stockpile you gain temporary hit points equal to your level. These temporary hit points are unique and can stack with other temporary hit points from Stockpile. These stacks last for only for the duration of this move and all disappear when the first stack runs out its duration. You may choose to lose all your stacks of Stockpile at any time. If you lose your stacks of stockpile for any reason you lose the AC and temporary hit points from this move.

#### Substitute
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You create a duplicate of yourself with one quarter of your HP (rounded down) which appears in your space as you disappear. This substitute has an AC of 1, speed of 0 feet, and takes all damage and status ailments you would normally take until it is destroyed. While the Substitute is in play your disappear into the Ethereal plane, becoming untargetable, and cannot move. You may attack as normal, with the substitute acting as yourself for the purposes of move's ranges. If the damage done is enough to destroy the substitute, you take the remaining damage and reappear in the substitute's place. If a creature ignores the effects of substitute they act as if you are in the space the substitute is in.

- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**

Each creature in that area must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failure, a creature takes 2d8 water damage and is knocked prone. On a success, a creature takes half as much damage and isn’t knocked prone. - **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You dance an odd, swaying, and a rhythmic dance. You may move up to your movement speed when you use Teeter Dance. While you move each creature within 10 feet of you must make a Wisdom saving throw, become confused on a failure. If any creature makes an attack of opportunity against you during this movement and misses that creature also becomes confused.

```

#### Telekinesis
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** Intelligence
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 500
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**  
You lift an object with your mind. When you use this move instead of spending PP normally you may spend PP from this move equal to the weight in pounds of the object you wish to lift. You may move that object up to 30 feet each round in any direction for the duration. If you wish to lift a creature, that creature can make an Intelligence saving throw against your MOVE DC to resist being lifted.

#### Teleport
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 2
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Description:**  
You use the power of your mind to instantaneously transport to another location. You may teleport to any location within range. It can be a place you can see, one you can visualize, or one you can describe by stating distance and direction, such as “200 feet straight downward” or “upward to the northwest at a 45-degree angle, 300 feet.” You can bring along objects as long as their weight does not exceed what you can carry. You can also bring one willing creature of your size or smaller who is carrying gear up to its carrying capacity. The creature must be within 5 feet of you when you cast this spell. If you would arrive in a place already occupied by an object or a creature, you and any creature traveling with you each take 4d6 force damage, and the spell fails to teleport you.
- **Higher Levels:**  
At level 5 the range of this move becomes 120 feet, at level 11 the range becomes 1000 feet, at level 17 the range becomes 5 miles.

#### Tickle
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 minute
- **Range:** Touch
- **Description:**  
You tickle an opponent until they laugh uncontrollably. Choose one opponent with range to make a Constitution saving throw against your MOVE DC. On a failure they begin to laugh and find everything funny, falling prone and being incapacitated for as long as the Tickle continues. On each of your turns until the duration of the move is over, you may use your bonus action to continue the Tickle if you are still within range of the target. If you do not continue the Tickle in this way, the effects of Tickle immediately end. Additionally, the target can retry the Constitution saving throw against your MOVE DC every time they take damage, ending the effect on a successful save.

- **PP:** 2
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Description:**

If they are in range the creature whose saving throw you failed makes a saving throw against whatever DC you failed, taking whatever effects happen on a success or failure. When they do so you suffer no ill effects of the move which triggered Topsy-Turvy.

#### Toxic Spikes
___
- **Type:** Poison
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 80 feet
- **Description:**  
You scatter a field of poisonous burrs across the ground. Choose one 30 foot square within range to be covered by the burrs. Each creature that moves 5 feet or more through the field must make a Constitution saving throw against your MOVE DC or become poisoned. If you have at least two fields of burrs overlapping, any creature that moves at least 5 feet through the overlapping fields suffers an even worse poison. They make a Constitution saving throw against your MOVE DC. On a failure they are poisoned and take double damage from the poison damage each turn. If a Pokémon is already poisoned while they move through the overlapping fields a failed Constitution save results in them exchanging their poisoned condition for this more harmful poison.

- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 reaction
- **PP:** 1
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Varies
- **Description:**

You must use this move before you know the result of any initiative rolls for this combat, including your own.

- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d10 at level 5, 2d6 at level 11, and 2d10 at level 17.

```

#### Whirlwind
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Wisdom/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self (15-foot sphere)
- **Description:**  
You create a whirlwind of spinning air around you. Each Pokémon within a 15 foot sphere center on yourself must make a Strength saving throw against your MOVE DC. On a failed save they are pushed 15 feet away from you and take 1d8 normal damage. On a successful saved they are not pushed and take half damage.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d12 at level 5, 2d8 at level 11, and 2d12 at level 17.

#### Wide Guard
___
- **Type:** Rock
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 reaction
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self (5-foot sphere)
- **Description:**  
You spread your arms to defend against a wide reaching move. When you are forced to make a saving throw against an effect that could affect multiple targets you may use Wide Guard as your reaction to give you and each creature of your choice within 5 feet of you advantage on that saving throw. If the triggering effect is damage and you or those creatures you select succeed on the saving throw, you take no damage from the attack as part of Wide Guard no matter the regular effects of the triggering attack.

#### Wild Charge
___
- **Type:** Electric
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 8
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You surround yourself in wildly spastic electric current before laying into your opponent. You may move up to 15 feet then make a melee attack roll, dealing 1d12 + MOVE electric damage on a hit. Using this move tuckers you out. Until the end of your next turn you move at half speed for all your movements.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d12 at level 5, 3d12 at level 11, and 4d12 at level 17.

#### Will-O-Wisp
___
- **Type:** Fire
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Wisdom
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 20
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You send out a ghostly wisp of flame which enters the foe's body. Make a ranged attack against an opponent, burning them on a hit.

#### Wing Attack
___
- **Type:** Flying
- **Move Power:** Strength/Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You strike out at an enemy Pokémon with your wings and the wind made by them. Make a ranged attack roll, doing 1d6 + MOVE flying damage on a hit.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d6 at level 5, 3d6 at level 11, and 4d6 at level 17.

#### Wish
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 1
- **Duration:** Varies (Concentration)
- **Range:** Varies
- **Description:**  
You pray that your dreams will come true. Yeah, me too buddy. Each time you use this move you may choose one of the following effects to happen: one ally within 1 mile regains 3d6 health, one enemy within 200 feet must make a DC 15 Charisma saving throw or take 3d6 non-typed damage, one ally within 200 feet gains +5 AC for 1 minute, or one ally within 200 feet has advantage on all skills checks, ability checks, and attack rolls for 10 minutes. If the effect you choose has a duration, you must concentrate on it for the duration.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 6d6 at level 5, 9d9 at level 11, and 12d6 at level 17.

#### Withdraw
___
- **Type:** Water
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 reaction
- **PP:** 8
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
When you are hit by a melee or ranged attack, you can use your reaction to use this move to increase your AC by +3 until the start of your next turn if it would cause that attack to miss.

#### Wonder Room
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 3
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Description:**  
You conjure a strange room full of symbols and warped imagery. Choose a 30 foot cube originating at a point within range for the pattern to momentarily appear in. Each creature in the area who sees the pattern must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failed save, the creature becomes charmed for the duration. While charmed by this spell, the creature is incapacitated and has a speed of 0. The effect ends for an affected creature if it takes any damage or if someone else uses an action to shake the creature out of its stupor.

#### Wood Hammer
___
- **Type:** Grass
- **Move Power:** Strength
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 7
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You bring down your arm in a slow powerful slam, aiming to smash your opponent. Make a melee attack roll against an opponent, dealing 2d12 + MOVE grass damage on a hit. Regardless of if you hit or miss this attack your reckless swing damages you own appendage. Until the end of your next turn you have disadvantage on melee attack rolls, move at half speed, and cannot take reactions.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 4d12 at level 5, 6d12 at level 11, and 8d12 at level 17.

#### Work Up
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 bonus action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** 1 minute (Concentration)
- **Range:** Self
- **Description:**  
You really amp yourself up! For the duration you have +1 to attack rolls and damage for both ranged and melee attacks. You cannot have this bonus from Work Up more then once.
- **Higher Levels:**  
At level 7 this bonus increases to +2 and at level 13 this bonus increases to +3.

#### Worry Seed
___
- **Type:** Grass
- **Move Power:** None
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 20
- **Duration:** 4 hours
- **Range:** Touch
- **Description:**  
You plant a seed with a faint odor and odd effect. Choose one creature you can touch to plant the seed on. For the duration the seed prevents the target from falling asleep. The seed is easy to dislodge and the target may do so as a bonus action.

#### Wrap
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Strength/Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You attempt to grapple a target into submission. Make a melee attack roll. On a hit, the target takes 1d4 + MOVE normal damage and is grappled and restrained by you. At the beginning of each of its turns, it may attempt to escape with a Strength saving throw against your Move DC. While a Pokémon is grappled by you you may continue this move, as a bonus action and without using a PP, to do an automatic 1d4 + MOVE damage.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 1d6 at level 5, 1d8 at level 11, and 1d10 at level 17.

- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 8
- **Duration:** Instantaneous

- **Higher Levels:**

#### Yawn
___
- **Type:** Normal
- **Move Power:** Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 5
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You yawn at your opponent, making them suddenly drowsy. Target one opponent within range that can see you. That target must move a Charisma saving throw against your MOVE DC. On a failure they gain the asleep condition at the start of their next turn. They cannot make a check to wake up on the same turn they fall asleep.

#### Zap Cannon
___
- **Type:** Electric
- **Move Power:** Intelligence/Charisma
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 6
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Description:**  
You charge a powerful bolt of arcing lightning, so powerful you can't quite control it. Make a ranged attack roll at disadvantage, dealing 1d12 + MOVE electric damage on a hit. If you hit with this move the target must make a Constitution saving throw against your MOVE DC or become paralyzed.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d12 at level 5, 3d12 at level 11, and 4d12 at level 17.

#### Zen Headbutt
___
- **Type:** Psychic
- **Move Power:** Strength/Intelligence
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 10
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You have a different method of delivering your head's psychic energy to your opponent. Make a melee attack roll against your opponent, dealing 1d10 + MOVE psychic damage on a hit. On a natural attack roll of 19 or 20 the target flinches.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d10 at level 5, 3d10 at level 11, and 4d10 at level 17.

#### Zing Zap
___
- **Type:** Electric
- **Move Power:** Strength/Dexterity
- **Move Time:** 1 action
- **PP:** 8
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Range:** Melee
- **Description:**  
You spin around and release your electricity through your quills. Make a melee attack roll against an opponent, dealing 1d10 + MOVE electric damage on a hit. On a natural roll of 17 or higher your quills are too prickly and you flinch your opponent.
- **Higher Levels:**  
The base damage of this attack increases to 2d10 at level 5, 3d10 at level 11, and 4d10 at level 17.
